000102c2 <simple_switch>:

	.text
	.global simple_switch
simple_switch:
	mov 4(%esp), %eax   // 取from->stack
   102c2:	8b 44 24 04          	mov    0x4(%esp),%eax
	mov 8(%esp), %edx   // 取to->stack
   102c6:	8b 54 24 08          	mov    0x8(%esp),%edx

	// 保存前一任务的状态
	push %ebp
   102ca:	55                   	push   %ebp
	push %ebx
   102cb:	53                   	push   %ebx
	push %esi
   102cc:	56                   	push   %esi
	push %edi
   102cd:	57                   	push   %edi

	// 切换栈
	mov %esp, (%eax)    // from->stack = esp
   102ce:	89 20                	mov    %esp,(%eax)
  
  	mov %edx, %esp      // esp = to->stack
   102d0:	89 d4                	mov    %edx,%esp
	// 加载下一任务的栈
	pop %edi
   102d2:	5f                   	pop    %edi
	pop %esi
   102d3:	5e                   	pop    %esi
	pop %ebx
   102d4:	5b                   	pop    %ebx
	pop %ebp
   102d5:	5d                   	pop    %ebp
  	ret
   102d6:	c3                   	ret

000102fb <write_cr3>:
	uint32_t cr2;
	__asm__ __volatile__("mov %%cr2, %[v]":[v]"=r"(cr2));
	return cr2;
}

static inline void write_cr3(uint32_t v) {
   102fb:	55                   	push   %ebp
   102fc:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp
    __asm__ __volatile__("mov %[v], %%cr3"::[v]"r"(v));
   102fe:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax
   10301:	0f 22 d8             	mov    %eax,%cr3
}

/**
 * @brief 初始化地址分配结构
 * 以下不检查start和size的页边界，由上层调用者检查
 */
static void addr_alloc_init (addr_alloc_t * alloc, uint8_t * bits,
                    uint32_t start, uint32_t size, uint32_t page_size) {

   103ac:	83 ec 08             	sub    $0x8,%esp

   103c1:	8b 55 10             	mov    0x10(%ebp),%edx
   103c4:	89 50 20             	mov    %edx,0x20(%eax)
    alloc->size = size;

   103ca:	8b 55 14             	mov    0x14(%ebp),%edx
   103cd:	89 50 24             	mov    %edx,0x24(%eax)
    alloc->page_size = page_size;

   103d3:	8b 55 18             	mov    0x18(%ebp),%edx
   103d6:	89 50 1c             	mov    %edx,0x1c(%eax)

   103dc:	8b 40 24             	mov    0x24(%eax),%eax

   103e4:	f7 75 18             	divl   0x18(%ebp)
   103e7:	89 c2                	mov    %eax,%edx
   103e9:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax
   103ec:	83 c0 14             	add    $0x14,%eax
   103ef:	6a 00                	push   $0x0

/**
 * 比较两个字符串，最多比较size个字符
 * 如果某一字符串提前比较完成，也算相同
 */
int kernel_strncmp (const char * s1, const char * s2, int size) {
   12b41:	55                   	push   %ebp
   12b42:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp
    if (!s1 || !s2) {

        return -1;

   12b55:	eb 66                	jmp    12bbd <kernel_strncmp+0x7c>
    }

    // 2023-3-18 这里size没有用到
    while (*s1 && *s2 && (*s1 == *s2) && size) {
    	s1++;
   12b57:	83 45 08 01          	addl   $0x1,0x8(%ebp)
    	s2++;

    	size--;
